1.5h-8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5Zm0 5h8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5Zm0 5h8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-8.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0-1.5ZM2 14a1 1 0 1 1 0-2 1 1 0 0 1 0 2Zm1-6a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 actions" title="More file actions" data-testid="more-file-actions-button" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 itGLhU prc-Button-ButtonBase-c50BI js-blob-dropdown-click prc-Button-IconButton-szpyj" data-loading="false" data-no-visuals="true" data-size="small" data-variant="invisible" aria-describedby=":Rnsptal9lab:-loading-announcement" 0 0-3 1.5 1.5 0 0 0 0 3Z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 hycJXc"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🚀 O Futuro do Desenvolvimento Web</h1><a id="user-content--o-futuro-do-desenvolvimento-web" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🚀 O Futuro do Desenvolvimento Web" href="https://github.com/alevitorio/exercicios-pwI/blob/main/pwI-lista-1.md#-o-futuro-do-desenvolvimento-web"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">O desenvolvimento web está em constante evolução, trazendo novas tecnologias e desafios. Criar um site moderno envolve conhecer diferentes linguagens e práticas recomendadas.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📌 Principais Tecnologias Utilizadas</h2><a id="user-content--principais-tecnologias-utilizadas" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📌 Principais Tecnologias Utilizadas" href="https://github.com/alevitorio/exercicios-pwI/blob/main/pwI-lista-1.md#-principais-tecnologias-utilizadas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">O desenvolvimento web pode ser dividido em três camadas principais:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Frontend</strong> – Responsável pela interface visual. Tecnologias principais:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>HTML (estrutura)</li>
<li>CSS (estilo)</li>
<li>JavaScript (interatividade)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f68746d6c2c6373732c6a617661736372697074"><img src="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f68746d6c2c6373732c6a617661736372697074" alt="Frontend" data-canonical-src="https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?html,css,javascript" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Backend</strong> – Responsável pelo funcionamento interno do site. Principais tecnologias:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Node.js</li>
<li>Python (Django, Flask)</li>
<li>PHP</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f7365727665722c6261636b656e64"><img src="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f7365727665722c6261636b656e64" alt="Backend" data-canonical-src="https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?server,backend" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Banco de Dados</strong> – Onde as informações são armazenadas. Alguns exemplos:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>MySQL</li>
<li>PostgreSQL</li>
<li>MongoDB</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔥 Tendências do Desenvolvimento Web</h2><a id="user-content--tendências-do-desenvolvimento-web" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔥 Tendências do Desenvolvimento Web" href="https://github.com/alevitorio/exercicios-pwI/blob/main/pwI-lista-1.md#-tend%C3%AAncias-do-desenvolvimento-web"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Algumas tendências estão moldando o futuro da web:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Aplicações Web Progressivas (PWA)</strong> – Sites que funcionam como apps nativos.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f6170702c70726f6772657373697665"><img src="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f6170702c70726f6772657373697665" alt="PWA" data-canonical-src="https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?app,progressive" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Inteligência Artificial</strong> – Personalização de experiências com IA.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f6172746966696369616c2c696e74656c6c6967656e6365"><img src="./README_files/68747470733a2f2f736f757263652e756e73706c6173682e636f6d2f343030783330302f3f6172746966696369616c2c696e74656c6c6967656e6365" alt="Inteligência Artificial" data-canonical-src="https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?artificial,intelligence" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Web 3.0 e Blockchain</strong> – Tecnologias descentralizadas para segurança e privacidade.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 Dicas para Iniciantes</h2><a id="user-content--dicas-para-iniciantes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 Dicas para Iniciantes" href="https://github.com/alevitorio/exercicios-pwI/blob/main/pwI-lista-1.md#-dicas-para-iniciantes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Se você está começando, siga estas etapas</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Aprenda HTML, CSS e JavaScript.</li>
<li>Pratique criando projetos simples.</li>
<li>Explore frameworks populares (React, Vue.js, Angular).</li>
<li>Entenda como funciona o backend.</li>
<li>Participe de comunidades e compartilhe seu código no GitHub.</li>
</ol>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💡 Como usar este conteúdo?</h3><a id="user-content--como-usar-este-conteúdo" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💡 Como usar este conteúdo?" href="https://github.com/alevitorio/exercicios-pwI/blob/main/pwI-lista-1.md#-como-usar-este-conte%C3%BAdo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Crie um arquivo <code>index.html</code> e copie o conteúdo abaixo para estruturar a página:</li>
</ol>

    &lt;h1&gt;🚀 O Futuro do Desenvolvimento Web&lt;/h1&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;O desenvolvimento web está em constante evolução, trazendo novas tecnologias e desafios...&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;img src=&quot;https://source.unsplash.com/800x400/?technology,code&quot; alt=&quot;Código em uma tela de computador&quot;&gt;

    &lt;h2&gt;📌 Principais Tecnologias Utilizadas&lt;/h2&gt;
    &lt;ol&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Frontend&lt;/strong&gt; – Responsável pela interface visual. Tecnologias principais:
            &lt;ul&gt;
                &lt;li&gt;HTML (estrutura)&lt;/li&gt;
                &lt;li&gt;CSS (estilo)&lt;/li&gt;
                &lt;li&gt;JavaScript (interatividade)&lt;/li&gt;
            &lt;/ul&gt;
            &lt;img src=&quot;https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?html,css,javascript&quot; alt=&quot;HTML, CSS e JavaScript&quot;&gt;
        &lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Backend&lt;/strong&gt; – Responsável pelo funcionamento interno do site...
            &lt;img src=&quot;https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?server,backend&quot; alt=&quot;Servidor backend&quot;&gt;
        &lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;

    &lt;h2&gt;🔥 Tendências do Desenvolvimento Web&lt;/h2&gt;
    &lt;ul&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;PWA&lt;/strong&gt; – Sites que funcionam como apps nativos.
            &lt;img src=&quot;https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?app,progressive&quot; alt=&quot;Aplicação web progressiva&quot;&gt;
        &lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;IA&lt;/strong&gt; – Personalização de experiências...
            &lt;img src=&quot;https://source.unsplash.com/400x300/?artificial,intelligence&quot; alt=&quot;Inteligência Artificial&quot;&gt;
        &lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ul&gt;

    &lt;h2&gt;🎯 Dicas para Iniciantes&lt;/h2&gt;
    &lt;ol&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;Aprenda HTML, CSS e JavaScript.&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;Pratique criando projetos simples.&lt;/li&gt;
        &lt;li&gt;Explore frameworks populares...&lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;
